  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3z7/Y0Ep52FLrh13mMD9l/dUPF5w98USN9/mm5+SM9fzJkGYB9OdJL4XW6QA8O2hkDbwj1wyOLd1cdOvyrHOow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9VUpzUToAnaIytAw7/hhG36avBKmExihQwvwHgl4VVrZTZc2AhJ4M31zluN3yHEtGfhww4rW5QQBpcUqXFuoLg==')})
  }

As leader of the band of light-fingered brothers known as the Gentleman Bastards, Locke is soon infamous, fooling even the underworld’s most feared ruler.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">About Brandon Sanderson</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1394044556p3/38550.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">Brandon Sanderson
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
154,099
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12965810522211885609">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent' title='The Dark Talent' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded' title='Arcanum Unbounded' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br/>Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul' title='The Emperor’s Soul' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Emperor’s S</a></i></span>
  <span id="freeText12965810522211885609" style="display:none">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent" title="The Dark Talent" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded" title="Arcanum Unbounded" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br />Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28698036.Mistborn__Secret_History" title="Mistborn: Secret History" rel="nofollow noopener">Mistborn: Secret History</a>,</i> and a brand-new Stormlight Archive novella, <i>Edgedancer</i>.<br /><br />Earlier this year he released <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704486.Calamity" title="Calamity" rel="nofollow noopener">Calamity</a>,</i> the finale of the #1 New York Times bestselling Reckoners trilogy that began with <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i>.<br /><br />Brandon Sanderson was born in 1975 in Lincoln, Nebraska. As a child Brandon enjoyed reading, but he lost interest in the types of titles often suggested to him, and by junior high he never cracked a book if he could help it. This changed when an eighth grade teacher gave him <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/176268.Dragonsbane" title="Dragonsbane" rel="nofollow noopener">Dragonsbane</a>
</i> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/10333.Barbara_Hambly" title="Barbara Hambly" rel="nofollow noopener">Barbara Hambly</a>.<br /><br />Brandon was working on his thirteenth novel when Moshe Feder at Tor Books bought the sixth he had written. Tor has published <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68427.Elantris" title="Elantris" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a>,</i> the Mistborn trilogy and its followup <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10803121.The_Alloy_of_Law" title="The Alloy of Law" rel="nofollow noopener">The Alloy of Law</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1268479.Warbreaker" title="Warbreaker" rel="nofollow noopener">Warbreaker</a>,</i> and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7235533.The_Way_of_Kings" title="The Way of Kings" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11543195.Words_of_Radiance" title="Words of Radiance" rel="nofollow noopener">Words of Radiance</a>,</i> the first two in the planned ten-volume series The Stormlight Archive. He was chosen to complete <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan" title="Robert Jordan" rel="nofollow noopener">Robert Jordan</a>’s Wheel of Time series; 2009’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.The_Gathering_Storm" title="The Gathering Storm" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gathering Storm</a>
</i> and 2010’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8253920.Towers_of_Midnight" title="Towers of Midnight" rel="nofollow noopener">Towers of Midnight</a>
</i> were followed by the final book in the series, <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.A_Memory_of_Light" title="A Memory of Light" rel="nofollow noopener">A Memory of Light</a>,</i> in January 2013. Four books in his middle-grade <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/623976.Alcatraz_vs__the_Evil_Librarians" title="Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians" rel="nofollow noopener">Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians</a>
</i> series have been released in new editions by Starscape, and his novella <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12796771.Infinity_Blade_Awakening" title="Infinity Blade Awakening" rel="nofollow noopener">Infinity Blade Awakening</a>
</i> was an ebook bestseller for Epic Games accompanying their acclaimed <i>Infinity Blade</i> iOS video game series. Two more novellas, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13452375.Legion" title="Legion" rel="nofollow noopener">Legion</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> were released by Subterranean Press and Tachyon Publications in 2012, and 2013 brought two young adult novels, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10137823.The_Rithmatist" title="The Rithmatist" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rithmatist</a>
</i> from Tor and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i> from Delacorte.<br /><br />The only author to make the short list for the David Gemmell Legend Award six times in four years, Brandon won that award in 2011 for <i>The Way of Kings</i>. <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> won the 2013 Hugo Award for Best Novella. He has appeared on the <i>New York Times</i> Best-Seller List multiple times, with five novels hitting the #1 spot.<br /><br />Currently living in Utah with his wife and children, Brandon teaches creative writing at Brigham Young University.</span>

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
